## release on 20260422
## description
## changes
⚡️ <strong>Rspack 2.0 Released!</strong> ⚡️

* 🚀 Read our <strong><a href="https://www.rspack.dev/blog/announcing-2-0" rel="nofollow">announcement blog post</a></strong> for new features, and highlights
* 🛠️ Check out the <strong><a href="https://www.rspack.dev/guide/migration/rspack_1.x" rel="nofollow">step-by-step migration guide</a></strong> for upgrading from v1 to v2
